# <a name="responsecode"></a><span data-ttu-id="4154e-103">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4154e-103">ResponseCode</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4154e-104">Das **ResponseCode** -Element enthält Statusinformationen über die Anforderung.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4154e-104">The **ResponseCode** element provides status information about the request.</span></span> 
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="4154e-105">ResponseMessage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4154e-105">ResponseMessage</span></span>](responsemessage.md) 
- [<span data-ttu-id="4154e-106">ResponseCode</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4154e-106">ResponseCode</span></span>](responsecode.md)
  
```XML
<ResponseCode/>
```

<span data-ttu-id="4154e-107">**ResponseCodeType**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4154e-107">**ResponseCodeType**</span></span>

## <a name="remarks"></a><span data-ttu-id="4154e-1480">Hinweise</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4154e-1480">Remarks</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="4154e-1481">Dieses Element ist nicht erforderlich, und ist nicht in allen Antworten enthalten.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4154e-1481">This element is not required and is not included in all responses.</span></span> 
  
<span data-ttu-id="4154e-1482">Das Schema, das dieses Element beschreibt, befindet sich im virtuellen IIS-Verzeichnis, das Exchange-Webdienste hostet.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4154e-1482">The schema that describes this element is located in the IIS virtual directory that hosts Exchange Web Services.</span></span>
